The prompt now includes a per-turn operating loop, explicit guard-state triage, expected-proof selection before editing, cross-lane blocker ledger guidance, dashboard/report update criteria, and a requirement-by-requirement completion ledger so future goal runs stay multi-lane and measurable instead of becoming open-ended useful-work loops.
- Added a goal-health check to `docs/autoresearch/active-options-performance-goal.md` so each future loop must report the active lane map, identify the one selected measurable slice, and state why untouched lanes are time-gated, artifact-blocked, or lower priority instead of silently drifting back to a single-lane audit.
- Fixed the tracked DB truth-health mismatch in `/api/options-profit/status`. The route still serves the stored options-profit status artifact for the proof gate, but now overlays `measurement_gate.checks.tracked_positions` from the current runtime positions repository used by `/api/positions`, including open/closed counts and proof-eligible realized metrics. Current-code FastAPI TestClient evidence reports `tracked_available=true`, `48` open positions, `488` total closed positions, and `1` proof-eligible realized closed row while the stored gate remains `blocked`. Updated the evidence module, tracked-position tab summary/filter copy, and focused Trading Desk evidence tests. ## 2026-05-31

- Redesigned the Trading Desk `Tracked Stocks` tab from a generic table into a compact stock watchlist. The view removes the bulky metric-card row, keeps a quiet inline summary, shows every tracked ticker once, groups open/closed/total counts, collapses lane families into capped chips with `+N` overflow, and keeps average P&L readable without a runaway horizontal table. Verification: `npm run lint`, `npm run verify:typecheck`, and in-app browser checks on `http://localhost:3000/` with no console warnings/errors.
- Cleaned up the Trading Desk closed-row table so it no longer exposes raw quote/review/exit-reason columns or reuses open-trade `Close now` status on closed positions. Closed tracked-position rows now show the smaller product-facing set: ticker, signal, trade, taken date, entry, exit price, realized P&L, and a plain `Closed` status with date; closed paper ideas received the same treatment. Verification: `npm run lint`, `npm run verify:typecheck`, and in-app browser desktop/mobile checks on `http://localhost:3000/` with no console warnings/errors.
- Removed the noisy tracked-trade diagnostic card stack from the Trading Desk Open/Closed view: evidence mix, lane-quality, and guardrail-readback panels no longer render on the primary board. Row-level evidence badges, summary stats, lane/date filters, and scanner/archive diagnostics remain available. Verification: `npm run lint`, `npm run verify:typecheck`, `npm run verify:docs`, and in-app browser desktop/mobile checks on `http://localhost:3002/` with no console warnings/errors; the temporary dev server was stopped after QA.
- Made the Trading Desk Closed Trades view accuracy-first by default. Closed rows now default to a truth-grade executable slice requiring an executable entry, trusted executable exit basis, realized P&L, and no lifecycle-only / proof-ineligible / legacy-unclassified provenance. Added Closed table evidence filters for truth-grade, all closed, historical paper, lifecycle-only, unpriced, and legacy rows, and changed closed summary cards to foreground truth-grade count, win rate, and average P&L while keeping research/backfill visible on demand. Verification: `npm run verify:typecheck` and `npm run lint`. A local dev server started on `http://localhost:3001` because `3000` was occupied, but browser automation could not run because the bundled Playwright package was missing `playwright-core`; the temporary dev server processes were stopped.
- Replaced the primary Trading Desk third tab with `Tracked Stocks`, a stock-level rollup of all tickers in the tracked-position store. The tab lists each tracked stock once with open/closed row counts, latest signal/trade dates, current open status, lane families, evidence mix, and average tracked P&L; the live scanner remains available under the archive toggle. Updated living docs for the new primary view shape. Verification: `npm run lint`, `npm run verify:typecheck`, `npm run verify:docs`, and in-app browser desktop/mobile checks on `http://localhost:3002/` with no console warnings/errors; the temporary dev server was stopped after QA.
- Simplified the Trading Desk tracked-position table so historical/paper rows no longer show target/stop/time-exit plan details. The tracked row now uses `Signal` for the entry lane family plus the signal date, moves Hold/Close-now into `Status`, and keeps the historical-paper provenance badge visible without the extra migrated-row detail line. Verification: `npm run lint`, `npm run verify:typecheck`, and in-app browser desktop/mobile checks on `http://localhost:3000/` with no console warnings/errors.
- Added a read-only Trading Desk exit-policy replay at `scripts/replay_trading_desk_exit_policies.py`, generated `docs/trading-desk-exit-policy-replay-2026-05-31.md`, `data/forward-tracking/trading_desk_exit_policy_replay_20260531T233603Z.json`, and latest JSON/CSV pointers, with tests in `tests/test_trading_desk_exit_policy_replay.py`. The replay uses stored executable review rows only and excludes unpriced/display-only/last-trade/midpoint rows. It found `107` replayable regular Trading Desk rows, baseline avg `+37.28%` and median `+35.79%`, and no promotable broad exit rule. Global profit harvest, global trailing giveback, shorter time exits, and stored-SELL following all reduced average executable P&L; `stop_70` and current-policy replay stayed research-only because they increased negatives and flipped stored winners to losses.
